#/_/gyi dgon pa na/_/smon lam dag pas rjes dang mjal/_/mkha' 'gros byin rlabs gnas lugs rtogs/_/mi pham mgon la phyag 'tshal lo/_/seng ge brag gi

ni|_rtog pa ci skyes kyang /_rig pa mig tu bcug pa'i tshul gyis/_mig 'bras mi 'gul ba la sems gtad de 'jog pa'o/_/gsum pa ni/_sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa gang byung yang //
de'i ngo bo la sems bzhag nas/_sngar gyi 'og rlung cung zad 'then pa'i lus yod du mi tshor ba'i bde ba de dang bsre'o/_/bzhi pa ni/_sems skad cig ma'i s+t+waMng du bde gsal mi

@#//sngar bzhin bsgom/_'dab ma re re'i s+t+waMng du/_e waM mA yA zhes pa 'od zer gyi rnam par bsgom s+t+waM/_gnyid du 'gro ba dang dus mtshungs par yig 'bru rnams

par spyod pa s+t+waM/_dpe ni byis pa bzhin no/_/bzhi pa ni/_tha mal gyi shes pa/_gnyug ma/_so ma/_lhug pa s+t+waM/_skye ba med pas gnyug ma/_gdod ma nas gnas pas tha mal gyi shes

@#//tsam la/_srid pa gsum dang dus gsum gyi bkod pa dang snang ba shar zhing /_sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams dpag tu med par phyin nas/_chos nyan pa sogs

@#/_/s+t+waMgs bu'i zhal gdams ni/

@#/_/sangs rgyas tshul bzhi'i zhal gdams/

!_/ma nor ma bcos bsam 'das brjod med ngang la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rna brgyud rin po che rdo rje zam pa 'di la gnyis te/_nag khrid dang /_dmar khrid gnyis so/_/nag 
khrid la don rnam pa gsum gyi skya bar nas brda' bzhi'i ngo sprod la brten nas bde gsal ngo sprad pa mun khung gi sgron me lta bu/_blo chung ba la lam du bstan no/_/dmar khrid la bzhi skor 
bsdoms kyi skya bar nas/_dus gsum gcig chod la brten nas/_gang shar thogs med du ngo sprad pas/_dper na sems can tshim pa lta bu/_de la rdo rje tshig lam sems kyi lde mig 
bstan pa 'di la/_rdo rje chos nyid kyi gshis brtan spros pa dang bral ba lam gyi gdams ngag bstan/_rang la gnas pa lde mig gis nyams su myong bar ngo sprad pas skye ba med pa'o//

sems dag lha'i bus/_slob dpon dga' rab rdo rje la skar ma rgyal gyi nyin par phyag spyi bor bzhag nas byin gyis brlabs pas/_a ha ho'i sgra byung bas yi ge 'bru bzhi la lam byas te 
bstan|_de'i don gsungs pa/_a skye ba med pa'i don bzhis bstan/_ha 'gyur ba med pa don gzer bzhis bstan/_ho 'gags pa med pa'i don brda' bzhis bstan/_'i dbyer mi phyed 
pa'i don bzhis bstan te/_a dbyings kyi tshul/_ye shes kyi tshul/_chos nyid kyi tshul/_bde ba'i tshul/_ha lta ba'i gzer/_sgom pa'i gzer/_spyod pa'i gzer/_'bras bu'i gzer bzhi'o//
ho dbang po ma bkag pa/_ma g.yos pa/_'og rlung 'then pa/_lce'i rtse mo gar yang mi brten/_'i tha mal gyi shes pa/_gnyug ma/_so ma/_lhug pa dang bzhi'o/_/sems nyid de dang po gang 
nas kyang ma byung bas/_skye ma myong bas chos nyid kyi tshul lo/_/tha ma gang du yang mi 'gro bas/_da lta skye mi srid pas dbyings kyi tshul/_da lta gang na yang mi gnas pas bde ba'i tshul/_de 
ye nas rang la yod par shes pas ye shes kyi tshul lo/_/sems nyid skye ma myong bas rnam rtog glo bur du byung yang /_dper na bya 'phur ba la/_rjes med pa ltar skyon gyis ma gos pa'o//

#/_/de mi skye bas nyon mongs dag_/bag chags dag_/skyon yul thon no/_/de ltar ngos bzung med pas/_cir yang lta bar 'char/_shar ba yang lta ba/_ma 'gags pas

pas|_sgom pa gtad med yengs med yin/_de tsam na snang ba ci shar cir snang yang shar ba ma 'gags 'dzin pa med/_ci shar rang sar dag pas/_dper na bya 'phur ba la rjes med

@#/_/zhal gdams 'phrul gyi me long dgu skor/
